RATING 	DEFINITION 	NOTE
(E) Exceptional 	Performance meets contractual
requirements and exceeds many to the
Government/Owner’s benefit. The
contractual performance of the
element or sub-element being
assessed was accomplished with few
minor problems for which corrective
actions taken by the contractor was
highly effective.
An Exceptional rating is appropriate
when the Contractor successfully
performed multiple significant events
that were of benefit to the
Government/Owner. A singular
benefit, however, could be of such
magnitude that it alone constitutes an
Exceptional rating. Also, there should
have been NO significant weaknesses
identified.
(VG) Very Good 	Performance meets contractual
requirements and exceeds some to the
Government’s/Owner’s benefit. The
contractual performance of the element
or sub-element being assessed was
accomplished with some minor
problems for which corrective actions
taken by the contractor were effective.
A Very Good rating is appropriate
when the Contractor successfully
performed a significant event that was
a benefit to the Government/Owner.
There should have been no significant
weaknesses identified.
(S) Satisfactory 	Performance meets minimum
contractual requirements. The
contractual performance of the element
or sub-element contains some minor
problems for which corrective actions
taken by the contractor appear or were
satisfactory.
A Satisfactory rating is appropriate
when there were only minor problems,
or major problems that the contractor
recovered from without impact to the
contract. There should have been NO
significant weaknesses identified. Per
DOD policy, a fundamental principle
of assigning ratings is that contractors
will not be assessed a rating lower
than Satisfactory solely for not
performing beyond the requirements
of the contract.
(M) Marginal 	Performance does not meet some
contractual requirements. The
contractual performance of the element
or sub-element being assessed reflects
a serious problem for which the
contractor has not yet identified
corrective actions. The contractor's
proposed actions appear only
marginally effective or were not fully
implemented.
A Marginal is appropriate when a
significant event occurred that the
contractor had trouble overcoming
which impacted the
Government/Owner.
(U) Unsatisfactory 	Performance does not meet most
contractual requirements and recovery
is not likely in a timely manner. The
contractual performance of the element
or sub-element contains serious
problem(s) for which the contractor's
corrective actions appear or were
ineffective.
An Unsatisfactory rating is appropriate
when multiple significant events
occurred that the contractor had
trouble overcoming and which
impacted the Government/Owner. A
singular problem, however, could be
of such serious magnitude that it alone
constitutes an unsatisfactory rating.
(N) Not Applicable 	No information or did not apply to your
contract
Rating will be neither positive nor
negative.

Client Information (Name):

=== SHEET: BOE ===
Regional Custodial Norfolk
Basis of Estimate
General Information:
Escalation Rate
• Escalation rate of 2.0% (1.02) used for estimating for Material, Equipment and on
site cost for 1st Option Period through 5th Award Option Period.
• Reference: Unified Facilities Criteria 3-701-01 DoD Facilities Pricing Guide for FY
2022 Operation and Maintenance Escalation Rates
• Unified Facilities Criteria 3-701-01 escalation rate for FY25 through FY30 equals
2.0%
Annex 0200000 Management and Administration
Overhead (on-site) - cost based on 7% of Total Direct Cost
• Seven estimated Firm-Fixed Price Management and Administration FTE’s (Refer to SCA -
Wage Determination worksheet).
• $329,142.02 estimated Firm Fixed Price Management and Administration burden cost
(Refer to SCA - Wage Determination worksheet).
• $329,142.02 is approximately 7% of Scoping Estimate.
• Refer to BMS B-14.11 Cost Estimating for FSC, Process Step 14.11.7 Determine Job
Overhead Cost
G&A - cost based on an average offered rate of 6% of total direct and overhead cost
• Refer to BMS B-14.11 Cost Estimating for FSC, Process Step 14.11.9 Summarize Cost and
Prices
Profit - cost based on an average offered rate of 6% of total direct and overhead cost not
including G&A
• Refer to BMS B-14.11 Cost Estimating for FSC, Process Step 14.11.9 Summarize Cost and
Prices
Sub-annex 1503010 Custodial
• Reference: RS Means Online Facilities Maintenance & International Sanitary Supply
Association (ISSA) utilized to determine direct labor hours
• Assumptions:
o Direct Labor Hours calculated for Prestige and Service Standard, CDC and Operational Areas
and include all maintenance requirements for each type of service
o Controleed Access based off 1 person for every = 20,500sqft based off historical data, 1
person = $4,817 per clearance NOTE: security clearances for Base Year ONLY
o Direct Material Cost = 20% of Direct Labor Cost
o Direct Equipment Cost = 15% of Direct Material Cost
• Comments inserted in cells for clarification as necessary
Prepared by:
Austen Jordan
FSC Regional Specification Writer
NAVFAC ML
9824 Virginia Avenue
Norfolk, Virginia 23511-3015
Voice: 757-341-0287

A700 VACUUM CARPETS / RUGS The Contractor vacuums carpeted areas, rugs, and walk-off mats
until they are free of all loose soil, debris, lint, dust, dirt, grit, ashes, staples, paper
clips, and other foreign matter. If walk off mats are present on a carpeted floor, remove mat,
vacuum where it was laying, replace mat to original location and vacuum the mat.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A701 SWEEP / DUST MOP FLOORS The Contractor sweeps and dust mops so as to present a
clean orderly soil free appearance with no loose dirt, hardened dirt, dust, smears, streaks,
paper, trash, or other debris.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A702 STRIPPING / REWAXING The Contractor sweeps or dust mops and strips resilient
flooring to remove all built-up wax and imbedded dirt prior to rewaxing. After application of
wax, the Contractor buffs floors or floor areas (if required) sufficiently for maximum gloss
and uniform sheen from wall to wall, including corners. The Contractor ensures that the
re-waxed floor presents a clean appearance free from scuff marks or dirt smears.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A703 DAMP / WET MOPPING The Contractor wet mops uncarpeted areas with approved cleaning
solutions. The detergent cleaner must adhere to environmental and natural resource conservation
requirements. Floors must be damp mopped to present a uniform appearance free of streaks, swirl
marks, detergent residue or evidence of soils stain, film, debris, standing water, or mop
strands.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A704 FLOOR FINISH The Contractor sweeps, or just mops floors, then wet mops the same
area, and after drying applies floor finish for equal and complete distribution throughout the
entire floor area. A uniform gloss without swirles or debris is expected.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A705 SPRAY BUFFING The Contractor sweeps, dust mops, wet mops, sprays area with a buffing
solution, buffs the floor area to a uniform floss leaving a equal and complete distribution
throughout the entire floor area.

-- 10 of 66 --

Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A706 CARPET / RUG SHAMPOO Prior to shampooing by the water extraction method, the
Contractor vacuums rugs and carpets free o f all loose soil and debris. The Contractor shampoos
carpets and rugs free of streaks, spots, and stains, and restores the carpet or rug to a bright
uniform color. After the carpet or rug dries, the Contractor returns furniture or other
equipment to their original positions.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A707 ROOM CLEANING The Contractor cleans all parts of the room surface up to a maximum
height or 10 feet. Wood surfaces are to be polished, upholstered furniture will be vacuumed,
both sides of doors are included. Marker board, chalkboards, chalk trays, and erasers, all
interior glass, plexiglass, glass lights located in walls, glass doors, glass wall, glass
partitions, etc. will be cleaned.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A708 REST ROOM CLEANING The Contractor cleans rest rooms so that everything within the
room is free from soil, stains, and odors. The appearance is clean, polished, and sanitary.
Work shall be completed within two calendar days after receipt of order.
A709 REST ROOMS SERVICE The Contractor shall fill dispensers and holders with rest room
supplies to their maximum capacity. Hand soaps shall be antibacterial, and rubber mat urinal
screens shall be dated. The Contracting Officer will be notified if holder, or dispensers are
damaged.
Work shall be completed within two calendar days after receipt of order.
A710 CLEANING LIGHT FIXTURES Globes, reflectors, covers, diffusers, and plastic side
panels shall be removed and washed. After cleaning and reassembling, light fixtures shall be
free of bugs, dirt, dust, streaks, grease, and other foreign matter.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A711 HIGH DUSTING/ CLEANING The Contractor removes all dust, lint, litter, from vertical
and horizontal surfaces above 10’-0" from floor level, including overhead piping. Light
fixtures, and ceiling areas. Contractor ensures walls are free of bugs, cobwebs, and loose
dirt.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A712 TRASH REMOVAL - INTERIOR The Contractor empties all trash from receptacles, boxes,
cartons within offices and corridors, ect. which are properly marked "trash" and dumps the
trash in the closest empty dumpster. Clear plastic liners will be installed on each receptacle.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A713 TRASH REMOVAL - EXTERIOR The Contractor empties all trash from exterior containers
up to 55 gallon, and picks-up loose trash within 10 foot around each container. Dump the trash
in the closest empty dumpster
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A714 CLEAN DRINKING FOUNTAIN The Contractor cleans fountain tops, spouts, plumbing,
hardware, and cabinet sides with a disinfectant approved for drinking fountains. Drinking
fountains shall present a clean appearance free of soil, markings, stains, streaks, and
watermarks.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A715 INTERIOR GLASS CLEANING The Contractor thoroughly cleans all interior glass
surfaces, window frames, sills, and sashes. The Contractor removes all adjacent surfaces wiped

-- 11 of 66 --

dry. The Contractor removes all paint, putty, film, and foreign matter found on glass surfaces.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A716 EXTERIOR GLASS CLEANING The Contractor thoroughly cleans all exterior glass
surfaces, window frames, sills, and sashes, from the ground line up to and including the second
floor to be free of streaks and stains, and wiped dry. The Contractor removes all paint, putty,
film, and foreign matter found on glass surfaces. Where storm windows exist, the contractor
cleans both sides of the storm window and the outside of the inner glass.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A717 CLEANING WINDOW BLINDS The Contractor removes and cleans window blinds free of all
dust and embedded dirt, and re-hangs the blinds in working order.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A718 EXTERIOR SWEEPING / POLICING The Contractor sweeps/polices exterior areas to present
a clean condition free from loose dirt, trash, and debris. Bag all that was sweeped/policed and
dump it in the nearest empty container.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A719 HOSE OFF EXTERIOR PORCHES, WALKS AND STEPS The Contractor hoses off front and rear
porch areas and connecting steps to remove dirt, debris and leaves.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A720 CLEAN UNDERNEATH RAISED COMPUTER FLOORS The Contractor removes sufficient floor
tiles and vacuums all exposed wires and floor area. Tiles will be reset when work is complete.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A721 CLEAN PARK BENCHES The Contractor cleans park benches to remove dirt, leaves and
other matter so the benches look clean and not unsightly.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A722 UPHOLSTERED FURNITURE CLEANING The Contractor cleans upholstered furniture so they
are free of loose soil, debris, lint, dust, and other matter. All spots and stains will be
cleaned in the process.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A723 REMOVING SNOW AND ICE The Contractor removes snow and ice from those building walks
ad entrances so that these areas are clean and safe for pedestrian traffic, and maintains the
areas free of snow and ice until 1800. The Contractor does not deposit shoveled/blown snow and
ice on common sidewalks being cleared by other station activities under any circumstances.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A724 CLEANING OF VENTILATION DIFFUSERS, GRILLES, AND VENTS Provide cleaning of
ventilation diffusers, grilles and vents by wiping with clean, cloth towels and if necessary
the Contracctor shall incorporate the use of approved solvents and cleaners to obtain the
desired results. The cleaning process shall remove all exterior dirt, dust and other unwanted
materials. The finished surfaces shall not be damage or scratched as a result of the cleaning
process.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A725 WATER EXTRACTION The Contractor shall remove water from interior building surfaces
where flooding has occurred due to pipe leaks, roof leaks, toilet overflow, and other various
sources of water intrusion. The interior building surfaces include all floor finishes. Removal
of water shall be performed in the most expeditious manner, by manual or mechanical means. The

-- 12 of 66 --

Contractor shall respond within four (4) hours of the order to proceed and work until the water
is removed. The Contractor shall provide drying fans in conjunction with water removal from all
carpeted surfaces and other surfaces as directed by the Contracting Officer.
The Contractor shall respond and be onsite ready to begin work within four hours after notice
to proceed. Work shall be completed within three calendar days.
A726 MOLD CLEANING Provide mold cleaning and removal (mold growth, mold stains, mold
odors) from wood and other cellulose-based building materials such as OSB board, drywall,
plaster, plywood, and ceiling tile as well as concrete and masonry surfaces such as bricks,
blocks, and poured concrete walls and floors. Other surfaces may include pipe insulation and
heating, ventilation, air conditioning (HVAC) insulation and ductwork surfaces. The locations
include interior building surfaces such as offices, mechanical equipment rooms, crawl spaces,
above suspended ceiling surfaces. All cleaning methods and materials shall be in conformance
with existing enviromental regulations and procedures.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A727 PROVIDE AND OPERATE AIR SCRUBBERS FOR MOLD CLEANING OPERATIONS The Contractor shall
provide air scrubber equipment when requested. A typical air scrubber includes a blower
assembly complete with HEPA filter, activated carbon filters and may include a germicidal UV-C
light. Air scrubbers are approved for use in removal of asbestos, lead, chemical fumes and
biological contaminants. Each order shall require the operation of one air scrubber for a
period of twenty-four (24) continuous hours of use. the Contractor shall provide power cords
required to reach the nearest power outlet.
The Contracting Officer may request the relocation of the air scrubber equipment within the
same 24 hour period and at no additional cost to the Government. Relocation is defined as "an
adjacent or adjoining room on the same floor of the building."
The Contractor shall place the equipment within eight (8) hours after receipt of order.
A728 PRESSURE WASHING Provide pressure washing services for exterior building surfaces.
The equipment pressure requirements (PSI) shall be determined by the necessity of the surface
to be cleaned. Typically this item will be used, but not limited to, cleaning of concrete
sidewalks, walkways, steps, ship piers and building exterior finishes such as brick, vinyl,
wood, concrete, stucco, EIFS (Exterior Insulation Finishing System). This will also include the
cleaning of areas around trash dumpsters. When necessary, the contractor shall also be required
to use approved cleaning chemicals that can be dispensed along with the pressure washing
process. The Contractor will be permitted to use the most convenient fresh water source located
at the work site as directed by the KO. The Contractor shall be required to provide sufficient
non-metallic water hoses to reach the water source.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A729 EMERGENCY CLEANING (Normal Working Hours) The Contractor shall provide emergency
cleaning services during normal working hours. Typical emergency cleaning services include
clean-up and removal of water from various surfaces due to plumbing or building leaks, removal
and clean up of broken ceiling tiles, broken glass, construction debris, dust, tracked in
mud/grease etc. The Contractor shall provide drying fans and other equipment as needed to
remove moisture from carpeting in a timely manner as to prevent mold growth and other damage
associated with moisture problems. Services may also include cleanup and removal of human
waste. This requirement will be noted on the order. The contractor shall perform the required
clean-up services at the same level as required for similar types of services set forth in
Spec. Item 3.1 of the Firm Fixed Price portion of the contract.
The Contractor shall respond within 1 hour after receipt of order and shall proceed until all
work is completed.
Services shall be ordered by the SF. Areas to be cleaned will be measured by the Government and

-- 13 of 66 --

confirmed by the Contractor.
A730 EMERGENCY CLEANING (Other Than Normal Working Hours) The Contractor shall provide
emergency cleaning services during other than normal working hours. Typical emergency cleaning
services include clean-up and removal of water from various surfaces due to plumbing or
building leaks, removal and clean up of broken ceiling tiles, broken glass, construction
debris, dust, tracked in mud/grease etc. The Contractor shall provide drying fans and other
equipment as needed to remove the moisture from carpeting in a timely manner as to prevent mold
growth and other damage associated with moisture problems. Services may also include cleanup
and removal of human waste. This requirement will be noted on the order. The contractor shall
perform the required clean-up services at the same level as required for similar types of
services set forth in Spec. Item 3.1 of the Firm Fixed Price portion of the contract.
The Contractor shall respond within 4 hours after receipt of order and shall proceed until all
work is completed.
Services shall be ordered by the SF. Areas to be cleaned will be measured by the Government and
confirmed by the Contractor.
A731 Disinfection of Frequently Touched Surfaces in Common Areas (Daily service for 30 day
period) The Contractor shall clean and disinfect fequently touched surfaces in common areas
to ensure surfaces are clean, sanitary, and free of potentially infectious materials. The
Contractor shall perform this task daily for a period of 30 days.
The Contractor shall clean and disinfect all frequently touched surfaces in common areas
(including lunch/break rooms), e.g., cabinets, chairs, copiers, countertops, doors, doorknobs,
handrails, elevator touch pads, ice machines, keyboards, light switches, microwave ovens,
monitors, phones, printers, refrigerators, shelving, shredders, tabletops, and vending
machines.
Common Areas include areas such as entryways, hallways, lobbies, lunch/break rooms, reception
areas, waiting rooms, conference rooms, elevators, and stairwells. >>
Surfaces shall be cleaned prior to disinfection, as instructed on the disinfectant
manufacturer s label. The Contractor shall ensure adequate contact time for effective
disinfection.
Cleaning agents used shall be EPA Approved for use against COVID-19. A list of EPA Approved
products is available at
https://www.epa.gov/pesticide-registration/list-n-disinfectants-use-against-sars-cov-2 or
https://www.americanchemistry.com/Novel-Coronavirus-Fighting-Products-List.pdf.

A733 Unit Priced Labor Work - MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide labor to perform all

A734 Material Costs- MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide all materials and equipment to

A700 VACUUM CARPETS / RUGS The Contractor vacuums carpeted areas, rugs, and walk-off mats
until they are free of all loose soil, debris, lint, dust, dirt, grit, ashes, staples, paper
clips, and other foreign matter. If walk off mats are present on a carpeted floor, remove mat,
vacuum where it was laying, replace mat to original location and vacuum the mat.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A701 SWEEP / DUST MOP FLOORS The Contractor sweeps and dust mops so as to present a
clean orderly soil free appearance with no loose dirt, hardened dirt, dust, smears, streaks,
paper, trash, or other debris.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A702 STRIPPING / REWAXING The Contractor sweeps or dust mops and strips resilient
flooring to remove all built-up wax and imbedded dirt prior to rewaxing. After application of
wax, the Contractor buffs floors or floor areas (if required) sufficiently for maximum gloss
and uniform sheen from wall to wall, including corners. The Contractor ensures that the
re-waxed floor presents a clean appearance free from scuff marks or dirt smears.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.

-- 20 of 66 --

A703 DAMP / WET MOPPING The Contractor wet mops uncarpeted areas with approved cleaning
solutions. The detergent cleaner must adhere to environmental and natural resource conservation
requirements. Floors must be damp mopped to present a uniform appearance free of streaks, swirl
marks, detergent residue or evidence of soils stain, film, debris, standing water, or mop
strands.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A704 FLOOR FINISH The Contractor sweeps, or just mops floors, then wet mops the same
area, and after drying applies floor finish for equal and complete distribution throughout the
entire floor area. A uniform gloss without swirles or debris is expected.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A705 SPRAY BUFFING The Contractor sweeps, dust mops, wet mops, sprays area with a buffing
solution, buffs the floor area to a uniform floss leaving a equal and complete distribution
throughout the entire floor area.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A706 CARPET / RUG SHAMPOO Prior to shampooing by the water extraction method, the
Contractor vacuums rugs and carpets free o f all loose soil and debris. The Contractor shampoos
carpets and rugs free of streaks, spots, and stains, and restores the carpet or rug to a bright
uniform color. After the carpet or rug dries, the Contractor returns furniture or other
equipment to their original positions.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A707 ROOM CLEANING The Contractor cleans all parts of the room surface up to a maximum
height or 10 feet. Wood surfaces are to be polished, upholstered furniture will be vacuumed,
both sides of doors are included. Marker board, chalkboards, chalk trays, and erasers, all
interior glass, plexiglass, glass lights located in walls, glass doors, glass wall, glass
partitions, etc. will be cleaned.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A708 REST ROOM CLEANING The Contractor cleans rest rooms so that everything within the
room is free from soil, stains, and odors. The appearance is clean, polished, and sanitary.
Work shall be completed within two calendar days after receipt of order.
A709 REST ROOMS SERVICE The Contractor shall fill dispensers and holders with rest room
supplies to their maximum capacity. Hand soaps shall be antibacterial, and rubber mat urinal
screens shall be dated. The Contracting Officer will be notified if holder, or dispensers are
damaged.
Work shall be completed within two calendar days after receipt of order.
A710 CLEANING LIGHT FIXTURES Globes, reflectors, covers, diffusers, and plastic side
panels shall be removed and washed. After cleaning and reassembling, light fixtures shall be
free of bugs, dirt, dust, streaks, grease, and other foreign matter.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A711 HIGH DUSTING/ CLEANING The Contractor removes all dust, lint, litter, from vertical
and horizontal surfaces above 10’-0" from floor level, including overhead piping. Light
fixtures, and ceiling areas. Contractor ensures walls are free of bugs, cobwebs, and loose
dirt.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A712 TRASH REMOVAL - INTERIOR The Contractor empties all trash from receptacles, boxes,
cartons within offices and corridors, ect. which are properly marked "trash" and dumps the

-- 21 of 66 --

trash in the closest empty dumpster. Clear plastic liners will be installed on each receptacle.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A713 TRASH REMOVAL - EXTERIOR The Contractor empties all trash from exterior containers
up to 55 gallon, and picks-up loose trash within 10 foot around each container. Dump the trash
in the closest empty dumpster
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A714 CLEAN DRINKING FOUNTAIN The Contractor cleans fountain tops, spouts, plumbing,
hardware, and cabinet sides with a disinfectant approved for drinking fountains. Drinking
fountains shall present a clean appearance free of soil, markings, stains, streaks, and
watermarks.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A715 INTERIOR GLASS CLEANING The Contractor thoroughly cleans all interior glass
surfaces, window frames, sills, and sashes. The Contractor removes all adjacent surfaces wiped
dry. The Contractor removes all paint, putty, film, and foreign matter found on glass surfaces.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A716 EXTERIOR GLASS CLEANING The Contractor thoroughly cleans all exterior glass
surfaces, window frames, sills, and sashes, from the ground line up to and including the second
floor to be free of streaks and stains, and wiped dry. The Contractor removes all paint, putty,
film, and foreign matter found on glass surfaces. Where storm windows exist, the contractor
cleans both sides of the storm window and the outside of the inner glass.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A717 CLEANING WINDOW BLINDS The Contractor removes and cleans window blinds free of all
dust and embedded dirt, and re-hangs the blinds in working order.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A718 EXTERIOR SWEEPING / POLICING The Contractor sweeps/polices exterior areas to present
a clean condition free from loose dirt, trash, and debris. Bag all that was sweeped/policed and
dump it in the nearest empty container.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A719 HOSE OFF EXTERIOR PORCHES, WALKS AND STEPS The Contractor hoses off front and rear
porch areas and connecting steps to remove dirt, debris and leaves.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A720 CLEAN UNDERNEATH RAISED COMPUTER FLOORS The Contractor removes sufficient floor
tiles and vacuums all exposed wires and floor area. Tiles will be reset when work is complete.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A721 CLEAN PARK BENCHES The Contractor cleans park benches to remove dirt, leaves and
other matter so the benches look clean and not unsightly.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A722 UPHOLSTERED FURNITURE CLEANING The Contractor cleans upholstered furniture so they
are free of loose soil, debris, lint, dust, and other matter. All spots and stains will be
cleaned in the process.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A723 REMOVING SNOW AND ICE The Contractor removes snow and ice from those building walks
ad entrances so that these areas are clean and safe for pedestrian traffic, and maintains the

-- 22 of 66 --

areas free of snow and ice until 1800. The Contractor does not deposit shoveled/blown snow and
ice on common sidewalks being cleared by other station activities under any circumstances.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A724 CLEANING OF VENTILATION DIFFUSERS, GRILLES, AND VENTS Provide cleaning of
ventilation diffusers, grilles and vents by wiping with clean, cloth towels and if necessary
the Contracctor shall incorporate the use of approved solvents and cleaners to obtain the
desired results. The cleaning process shall remove all exterior dirt, dust and other unwanted
materials. The finished surfaces shall not be damage or scratched as a result of the cleaning
process.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A725 WATER EXTRACTION The Contractor shall remove water from interior building surfaces
where flooding has occurred due to pipe leaks, roof leaks, toilet overflow, and other various
sources of water intrusion. The interior building surfaces include all floor finishes. Removal
of water shall be performed in the most expeditious manner, by manual or mechanical means. The
Contractor shall respond within four (4) hours of the order to proceed and work until the water
is removed. The Contractor shall provide drying fans in conjunction with water removal from all
carpeted surfaces and other surfaces as directed by the Contracting Officer.
The Contractor shall respond and be onsite ready to begin work within four hours after notice
to proceed. Work shall be completed within three calendar days.
A726 MOLD CLEANING Provide mold cleaning and removal (mold growth, mold stains, mold
odors) from wood and other cellulose-based building materials such as OSB board, drywall,
plaster, plywood, and ceiling tile as well as concrete and masonry surfaces such as bricks,
blocks, and poured concrete walls and floors. Other surfaces may include pipe insulation and
heating, ventilation, air conditioning (HVAC) insulation and ductwork surfaces. The locations
include interior building surfaces such as offices, mechanical equipment rooms, crawl spaces,
above suspended ceiling surfaces. All cleaning methods and materials shall be in conformance
with existing enviromental regulations and procedures.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A727 PROVIDE AND OPERATE AIR SCRUBBERS FOR MOLD CLEANING OPERATIONS The Contractor shall
provide air scrubber equipment when requested. A typical air scrubber includes a blower
assembly complete with HEPA filter, activated carbon filters and may include a germicidal UV-C
light. Air scrubbers are approved for use in removal of asbestos, lead, chemical fumes and
biological contaminants. Each order shall require the operation of one air scrubber for a
period of twenty-four (24) continuous hours of use. the Contractor shall provide power cords
required to reach the nearest power outlet.
The Contracting Officer may request the relocation of the air scrubber equipment within the
same 24 hour period and at no additional cost to the Government. Relocation is defined as "an
adjacent or adjoining room on the same floor of the building."
The Contractor shall place the equipment within eight (8) hours after receipt of order.
A728 PRESSURE WASHING Provide pressure washing services for exterior building surfaces.
The equipment pressure requirements (PSI) shall be determined by the necessity of the surface
to be cleaned. Typically this item will be used, but not limited to, cleaning of concrete
sidewalks, walkways, steps, ship piers and building exterior finishes such as brick, vinyl,
wood, concrete, stucco, EIFS (Exterior Insulation Finishing System). This will also include the
cleaning of areas around trash dumpsters. When necessary, the contractor shall also be required
to use approved cleaning chemicals that can be dispensed along with the pressure washing
process. The Contractor will be permitted to use the most convenient fresh water source located
at the work site as directed by the KO. The Contractor shall be required to provide sufficient
non-metallic water hoses to reach the water source.

-- 23 of 66 --

Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A729 EMERGENCY CLEANING (Normal Working Hours) The Contractor shall provide emergency
cleaning services during normal working hours. Typical emergency cleaning services include
clean-up and removal of water from various surfaces due to plumbing or building leaks, removal
and clean up of broken ceiling tiles, broken glass, construction debris, dust, tracked in
mud/grease etc. The Contractor shall provide drying fans and other equipment as needed to
remove moisture from carpeting in a timely manner as to prevent mold growth and other damage
associated with moisture problems. Services may also include cleanup and removal of human
waste. This requirement will be noted on the order. The contractor shall perform the required
clean-up services at the same level as required for similar types of services set forth in
Spec. Item 3.1 of the Firm Fixed Price portion of the contract.
The Contractor shall respond within 1 hour after receipt of order and shall proceed until all
work is completed.
Services shall be ordered by the SF. Areas to be cleaned will be measured by the Government and
confirmed by the Contractor.
A730 EMERGENCY CLEANING (Other Than Normal Working Hours) The Contractor shall provide
emergency cleaning services during other than normal working hours. Typical emergency cleaning
services include clean-up and removal of water from various surfaces due to plumbing or
building leaks, removal and clean up of broken ceiling tiles, broken glass, construction
debris, dust, tracked in mud/grease etc. The Contractor shall provide drying fans and other
equipment as needed to remove the moisture from carpeting in a timely manner as to prevent mold
growth and other damage associated with moisture problems. Services may also include cleanup
and removal of human waste. This requirement will be noted on the order. The contractor shall
perform the required clean-up services at the same level as required for similar types of
services set forth in Spec. Item 3.1 of the Firm Fixed Price portion of the contract.
The Contractor shall respond within 4 hours after receipt of order and shall proceed until all
work is completed.
Services shall be ordered by the SF. Areas to be cleaned will be measured by the Government and
confirmed by the Contractor.
A731 Disinfection of Frequently Touched Surfaces in Common Areas (Daily service for 30 day
period) The Contractor shall clean and disinfect fequently touched surfaces in common areas
to ensure surfaces are clean, sanitary, and free of potentially infectious materials. The
Contractor shall perform this task daily for a period of 30 days.
The Contractor shall clean and disinfect all frequently touched surfaces in common areas
(including lunch/break rooms), e.g., cabinets, chairs, copiers, countertops, doors, doorknobs,
handrails, elevator touch pads, ice machines, keyboards, light switches, microwave ovens,
monitors, phones, printers, refrigerators, shelving, shredders, tabletops, and vending
machines.
Common Areas include areas such as entryways, hallways, lobbies, lunch/break rooms, reception
areas, waiting rooms, conference rooms, elevators, and stairwells. >>
Surfaces shall be cleaned prior to disinfection, as instructed on the disinfectant
manufacturer s label. The Contractor shall ensure adequate contact time for effective
disinfection.
Cleaning agents used shall be EPA Approved for use against COVID-19. A list of EPA Approved
products is available at

-- 24 of 66 --

https://www.epa.gov/pesticide-registration/list-n-disinfectants-use-against-sars-cov-2 or
https://www.americanchemistry.com/Novel-Coronavirus-Fighting-Products-List.pdf.
A732 Unit Priced Labor Work - MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide labor to perform all
Unit Priced Labor work subject to the Service Contract Act per the scope and delivery schedule
specified in the order.
A733 Unit Priced Labor Work - MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide labor to perform all
Unit Priced Labor work subject to the Collective Bargaining Agreement per the scope and
delivery schedule specified in the order.
A734 Material Costs- MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide all materials and equipment to
perform Unit Priced Labor work per the scope and delivery schedule specified in the order.

A700 VACUUM CARPETS / RUGS The Contractor vacuums carpeted areas, rugs, and walk-off mats
until they are free of all loose soil, debris, lint, dust, dirt, grit, ashes, staples, paper
clips, and other foreign matter. If walk off mats are present on a carpeted floor, remove mat,

-- 30 of 66 --

vacuum where it was laying, replace mat to original location and vacuum the mat.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A701 SWEEP / DUST MOP FLOORS The Contractor sweeps and dust mops so as to present a
clean orderly soil free appearance with no loose dirt, hardened dirt, dust, smears, streaks,
paper, trash, or other debris.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A702 STRIPPING / REWAXING The Contractor sweeps or dust mops and strips resilient
flooring to remove all built-up wax and imbedded dirt prior to rewaxing. After application of
wax, the Contractor buffs floors or floor areas (if required) sufficiently for maximum gloss
and uniform sheen from wall to wall, including corners. The Contractor ensures that the
re-waxed floor presents a clean appearance free from scuff marks or dirt smears.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A703 DAMP / WET MOPPING The Contractor wet mops uncarpeted areas with approved cleaning
solutions. The detergent cleaner must adhere to environmental and natural resource conservation
requirements. Floors must be damp mopped to present a uniform appearance free of streaks, swirl
marks, detergent residue or evidence of soils stain, film, debris, standing water, or mop
strands.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A704 FLOOR FINISH The Contractor sweeps, or just mops floors, then wet mops the same
area, and after drying applies floor finish for equal and complete distribution throughout the
entire floor area. A uniform gloss without swirles or debris is expected.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A705 SPRAY BUFFING The Contractor sweeps, dust mops, wet mops, sprays area with a buffing
solution, buffs the floor area to a uniform floss leaving a equal and complete distribution
throughout the entire floor area.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A706 CARPET / RUG SHAMPOO Prior to shampooing by the water extraction method, the
Contractor vacuums rugs and carpets free o f all loose soil and debris. The Contractor shampoos
carpets and rugs free of streaks, spots, and stains, and restores the carpet or rug to a bright
uniform color. After the carpet or rug dries, the Contractor returns furniture or other
equipment to their original positions.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A707 ROOM CLEANING The Contractor cleans all parts of the room surface up to a maximum
height or 10 feet. Wood surfaces are to be polished, upholstered furniture will be vacuumed,
both sides of doors are included. Marker board, chalkboards, chalk trays, and erasers, all
interior glass, plexiglass, glass lights located in walls, glass doors, glass wall, glass
partitions, etc. will be cleaned.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A708 REST ROOM CLEANING The Contractor cleans rest rooms so that everything within the
room is free from soil, stains, and odors. The appearance is clean, polished, and sanitary.
Work shall be completed within two calendar days after receipt of order.
A709 REST ROOMS SERVICE The Contractor shall fill dispensers and holders with rest room
supplies to their maximum capacity. Hand soaps shall be antibacterial, and rubber mat urinal
screens shall be dated. The Contracting Officer will be notified if holder, or dispensers are

-- 31 of 66 --

damaged.
Work shall be completed within two calendar days after receipt of order.
A710 CLEANING LIGHT FIXTURES Globes, reflectors, covers, diffusers, and plastic side
panels shall be removed and washed. After cleaning and reassembling, light fixtures shall be
free of bugs, dirt, dust, streaks, grease, and other foreign matter.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A711 HIGH DUSTING/ CLEANING The Contractor removes all dust, lint, litter, from vertical
and horizontal surfaces above 10’-0" from floor level, including overhead piping. Light
fixtures, and ceiling areas. Contractor ensures walls are free of bugs, cobwebs, and loose
dirt.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A712 TRASH REMOVAL - INTERIOR The Contractor empties all trash from receptacles, boxes,
cartons within offices and corridors, ect. which are properly marked "trash" and dumps the
trash in the closest empty dumpster. Clear plastic liners will be installed on each receptacle.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A713 TRASH REMOVAL - EXTERIOR The Contractor empties all trash from exterior containers
up to 55 gallon, and picks-up loose trash within 10 foot around each container. Dump the trash
in the closest empty dumpster
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A714 CLEAN DRINKING FOUNTAIN The Contractor cleans fountain tops, spouts, plumbing,
hardware, and cabinet sides with a disinfectant approved for drinking fountains. Drinking
fountains shall present a clean appearance free of soil, markings, stains, streaks, and
watermarks.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A715 INTERIOR GLASS CLEANING The Contractor thoroughly cleans all interior glass
surfaces, window frames, sills, and sashes. The Contractor removes all adjacent surfaces wiped
dry. The Contractor removes all paint, putty, film, and foreign matter found on glass surfaces.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A716 EXTERIOR GLASS CLEANING The Contractor thoroughly cleans all exterior glass
surfaces, window frames, sills, and sashes, from the ground line up to and including the second
floor to be free of streaks and stains, and wiped dry. The Contractor removes all paint, putty,
film, and foreign matter found on glass surfaces. Where storm windows exist, the contractor
cleans both sides of the storm window and the outside of the inner glass.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A717 CLEANING WINDOW BLINDS The Contractor removes and cleans window blinds free of all
dust and embedded dirt, and re-hangs the blinds in working order.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A718 EXTERIOR SWEEPING / POLICING The Contractor sweeps/polices exterior areas to present
a clean condition free from loose dirt, trash, and debris. Bag all that was sweeped/policed and
dump it in the nearest empty container.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A719 HOSE OFF EXTERIOR PORCHES, WALKS AND STEPS The Contractor hoses off front and rear
porch areas and connecting steps to remove dirt, debris and leaves.

-- 32 of 66 --

Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A720 CLEAN UNDERNEATH RAISED COMPUTER FLOORS The Contractor removes sufficient floor
tiles and vacuums all exposed wires and floor area. Tiles will be reset when work is complete.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A721 CLEAN PARK BENCHES The Contractor cleans park benches to remove dirt, leaves and
other matter so the benches look clean and not unsightly.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A722 UPHOLSTERED FURNITURE CLEANING The Contractor cleans upholstered furniture so they
are free of loose soil, debris, lint, dust, and other matter. All spots and stains will be
cleaned in the process.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A723 REMOVING SNOW AND ICE The Contractor removes snow and ice from those building walks
ad entrances so that these areas are clean and safe for pedestrian traffic, and maintains the
areas free of snow and ice until 1800. The Contractor does not deposit shoveled/blown snow and
ice on common sidewalks being cleared by other station activities under any circumstances.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A724 CLEANING OF VENTILATION DIFFUSERS, GRILLES, AND VENTS Provide cleaning of
ventilation diffusers, grilles and vents by wiping with clean, cloth towels and if necessary
the Contracctor shall incorporate the use of approved solvents and cleaners to obtain the
desired results. The cleaning process shall remove all exterior dirt, dust and other unwanted
materials. The finished surfaces shall not be damage or scratched as a result of the cleaning
process.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A725 WATER EXTRACTION The Contractor shall remove water from interior building surfaces
where flooding has occurred due to pipe leaks, roof leaks, toilet overflow, and other various
sources of water intrusion. The interior building surfaces include all floor finishes. Removal
of water shall be performed in the most expeditious manner, by manual or mechanical means. The
Contractor shall respond within four (4) hours of the order to proceed and work until the water
is removed. The Contractor shall provide drying fans in conjunction with water removal from all
carpeted surfaces and other surfaces as directed by the Contracting Officer.
The Contractor shall respond and be onsite ready to begin work within four hours after notice
to proceed. Work shall be completed within three calendar days.
A726 MOLD CLEANING Provide mold cleaning and removal (mold growth, mold stains, mold
odors) from wood and other cellulose-based building materials such as OSB board, drywall,
plaster, plywood, and ceiling tile as well as concrete and masonry surfaces such as bricks,
blocks, and poured concrete walls and floors. Other surfaces may include pipe insulation and
heating, ventilation, air conditioning (HVAC) insulation and ductwork surfaces. The locations
include interior building surfaces such as offices, mechanical equipment rooms, crawl spaces,
above suspended ceiling surfaces. All cleaning methods and materials shall be in conformance
with existing enviromental regulations and procedures.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A727 PROVIDE AND OPERATE AIR SCRUBBERS FOR MOLD CLEANING OPERATIONS The Contractor shall
provide air scrubber equipment when requested. A typical air scrubber includes a blower
assembly complete with HEPA filter, activated carbon filters and may include a germicidal UV-C
light. Air scrubbers are approved for use in removal of asbestos, lead, chemical fumes and
biological contaminants. Each order shall require the operation of one air scrubber for a
period of twenty-four (24) continuous hours of use. the Contractor shall provide power cords

-- 33 of 66 --

required to reach the nearest power outlet.
The Contracting Officer may request the relocation of the air scrubber equipment within the
same 24 hour period and at no additional cost to the Government. Relocation is defined as "an
adjacent or adjoining room on the same floor of the building."
The Contractor shall place the equipment within eight (8) hours after receipt of order.
A728 PRESSURE WASHING Provide pressure washing services for exterior building surfaces.
The equipment pressure requirements (PSI) shall be determined by the necessity of the surface
to be cleaned. Typically this item will be used, but not limited to, cleaning of concrete
sidewalks, walkways, steps, ship piers and building exterior finishes such as brick, vinyl,
wood, concrete, stucco, EIFS (Exterior Insulation Finishing System). This will also include the
cleaning of areas around trash dumpsters. When necessary, the contractor shall also be required
to use approved cleaning chemicals that can be dispensed along with the pressure washing
process. The Contractor will be permitted to use the most convenient fresh water source located
at the work site as directed by the KO. The Contractor shall be required to provide sufficient
non-metallic water hoses to reach the water source.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A729 EMERGENCY CLEANING (Normal Working Hours) The Contractor shall provide emergency
cleaning services during normal working hours. Typical emergency cleaning services include
clean-up and removal of water from various surfaces due to plumbing or building leaks, removal
and clean up of broken ceiling tiles, broken glass, construction debris, dust, tracked in
mud/grease etc. The Contractor shall provide drying fans and other equipment as needed to
remove moisture from carpeting in a timely manner as to prevent mold growth and other damage
associated with moisture problems. Services may also include cleanup and removal of human
waste. This requirement will be noted on the order. The contractor shall perform the required
clean-up services at the same level as required for similar types of services set forth in
Spec. Item 3.1 of the Firm Fixed Price portion of the contract.
The Contractor shall respond within 1 hour after receipt of order and shall proceed until all
work is completed.
Services shall be ordered by the SF. Areas to be cleaned will be measured by the Government and
confirmed by the Contractor.
A730 EMERGENCY CLEANING (Other Than Normal Working Hours) The Contractor shall provide
emergency cleaning services during other than normal working hours. Typical emergency cleaning
services include clean-up and removal of water from various surfaces due to plumbing or
building leaks, removal and clean up of broken ceiling tiles, broken glass, construction
debris, dust, tracked in mud/grease etc. The Contractor shall provide drying fans and other
equipment as needed to remove the moisture from carpeting in a timely manner as to prevent mold
growth and other damage associated with moisture problems. Services may also include cleanup
and removal of human waste. This requirement will be noted on the order. The contractor shall
perform the required clean-up services at the same level as required for similar types of
services set forth in Spec. Item 3.1 of the Firm Fixed Price portion of the contract.
The Contractor shall respond within 4 hours after receipt of order and shall proceed until all
work is completed.
Services shall be ordered by the SF. Areas to be cleaned will be measured by the Government and
confirmed by the Contractor.
A731 Disinfection of Frequently Touched Surfaces in Common Areas (Daily service for 30 day
period) The Contractor shall clean and disinfect fequently touched surfaces in common areas
to ensure surfaces are clean, sanitary, and free of potentially infectious materials. The
Contractor shall perform this task daily for a period of 30 days.
The Contractor shall clean and disinfect all frequently touched surfaces in common areas

-- 34 of 66 --

(including lunch/break rooms), e.g., cabinets, chairs, copiers, countertops, doors, doorknobs,
handrails, elevator touch pads, ice machines, keyboards, light switches, microwave ovens,
monitors, phones, printers, refrigerators, shelving, shredders, tabletops, and vending
machines.
Common Areas include areas such as entryways, hallways, lobbies, lunch/break rooms, reception
areas, waiting rooms, conference rooms, elevators, and stairwells. >>
Surfaces shall be cleaned prior to disinfection, as instructed on the disinfectant
manufacturer s label. The Contractor shall ensure adequate contact time for effective
disinfection.
Cleaning agents used shall be EPA Approved for use against COVID-19. A list of EPA Approved
products is available at
https://www.epa.gov/pesticide-registration/list-n-disinfectants-use-against-sars-cov-2 or
https://www.americanchemistry.com/Novel-Coronavirus-Fighting-Products-List.pdf.
A732 Unit Priced Labor Work - MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide labor to perform all
Unit Priced Labor work subject to the Service Contract Act per the scope and delivery schedule
specified in the order.
A733 Unit Priced Labor Work - MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide labor to perform all
Unit Priced Labor work subject to the Collective Bargaining Agreement per the scope and
delivery schedule specified in the order.
A734 Material Costs- MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide all materials and equipment to
perform Unit Priced Labor work per the scope and delivery schedule specified in the order.

A700 VACUUM CARPETS / RUGS The Contractor vacuums carpeted areas, rugs, and walk-off mats
until they are free of all loose soil, debris, lint, dust, dirt, grit, ashes, staples, paper
clips, and other foreign matter. If walk off mats are present on a carpeted floor, remove mat,
vacuum where it was laying, replace mat to original location and vacuum the mat.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A701 SWEEP / DUST MOP FLOORS The Contractor sweeps and dust mops so as to present a
clean orderly soil free appearance with no loose dirt, hardened dirt, dust, smears, streaks,
paper, trash, or other debris.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A702 STRIPPING / REWAXING The Contractor sweeps or dust mops and strips resilient
flooring to remove all built-up wax and imbedded dirt prior to rewaxing. After application of
wax, the Contractor buffs floors or floor areas (if required) sufficiently for maximum gloss
and uniform sheen from wall to wall, including corners. The Contractor ensures that the
re-waxed floor presents a clean appearance free from scuff marks or dirt smears.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A703 DAMP / WET MOPPING The Contractor wet mops uncarpeted areas with approved cleaning
solutions. The detergent cleaner must adhere to environmental and natural resource conservation
requirements. Floors must be damp mopped to present a uniform appearance free of streaks, swirl
marks, detergent residue or evidence of soils stain, film, debris, standing water, or mop
strands.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A704 FLOOR FINISH The Contractor sweeps, or just mops floors, then wet mops the same
area, and after drying applies floor finish for equal and complete distribution throughout the
entire floor area. A uniform gloss without swirles or debris is expected.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A705 SPRAY BUFFING The Contractor sweeps, dust mops, wet mops, sprays area with a buffing
solution, buffs the floor area to a uniform floss leaving a equal and complete distribution
throughout the entire floor area.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A706 CARPET / RUG SHAMPOO Prior to shampooing by the water extraction method, the
Contractor vacuums rugs and carpets free o f all loose soil and debris. The Contractor shampoos
carpets and rugs free of streaks, spots, and stains, and restores the carpet or rug to a bright
uniform color. After the carpet or rug dries, the Contractor returns furniture or other
equipment to their original positions.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A707 ROOM CLEANING The Contractor cleans all parts of the room surface up to a maximum

-- 41 of 66 --

height or 10 feet. Wood surfaces are to be polished, upholstered furniture will be vacuumed,
both sides of doors are included. Marker board, chalkboards, chalk trays, and erasers, all
interior glass, plexiglass, glass lights located in walls, glass doors, glass wall, glass
partitions, etc. will be cleaned.
Work shall be completed within four calendar days after receipt of order.
A708 REST ROOM CLEANING The Contractor cleans rest rooms so that everything within the
room is free from soil, stains, and odors. The appearance is clean, polished, and sanitary.
Work shall be completed within two calendar days after receipt of order.
A709 REST ROOMS SERVICE The Contractor shall fill dispensers and holders with rest room
supplies to their maximum capacity. Hand soaps shall be antibacterial, and rubber mat urinal
screens shall be dated. The Contracting Officer will be notified if holder, or dispensers are
damaged.
Work shall be completed within two calendar days after receipt of order.
A710 CLEANING LIGHT FIXTURES Globes, reflectors, covers, diffusers, and plastic side
panels shall be removed and washed. After cleaning and reassembling, light fixtures shall be
free of bugs, dirt, dust, streaks, grease, and other foreign matter.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A711 HIGH DUSTING/ CLEANING The Contractor removes all dust, lint, litter, from vertical
and horizontal surfaces above 10’-0" from floor level, including overhead piping. Light
fixtures, and ceiling areas. Contractor ensures walls are free of bugs, cobwebs, and loose
dirt.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A712 TRASH REMOVAL - INTERIOR The Contractor empties all trash from receptacles, boxes,
cartons within offices and corridors, ect. which are properly marked "trash" and dumps the
trash in the closest empty dumpster. Clear plastic liners will be installed on each receptacle.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A713 TRASH REMOVAL - EXTERIOR The Contractor empties all trash from exterior containers
up to 55 gallon, and picks-up loose trash within 10 foot around each container. Dump the trash
in the closest empty dumpster
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A714 CLEAN DRINKING FOUNTAIN The Contractor cleans fountain tops, spouts, plumbing,
hardware, and cabinet sides with a disinfectant approved for drinking fountains. Drinking
fountains shall present a clean appearance free of soil, markings, stains, streaks, and
watermarks.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A715 INTERIOR GLASS CLEANING The Contractor thoroughly cleans all interior glass
surfaces, window frames, sills, and sashes. The Contractor removes all adjacent surfaces wiped
dry. The Contractor removes all paint, putty, film, and foreign matter found on glass surfaces.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A716 EXTERIOR GLASS CLEANING The Contractor thoroughly cleans all exterior glass
surfaces, window frames, sills, and sashes, from the ground line up to and including the second
floor to be free of streaks and stains, and wiped dry. The Contractor removes all paint, putty,
film, and foreign matter found on glass surfaces. Where storm windows exist, the contractor
cleans both sides of the storm window and the outside of the inner glass.

-- 42 of 66 --

Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A717 CLEANING WINDOW BLINDS The Contractor removes and cleans window blinds free of all
dust and embedded dirt, and re-hangs the blinds in working order.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A718 EXTERIOR SWEEPING / POLICING The Contractor sweeps/polices exterior areas to present
a clean condition free from loose dirt, trash, and debris. Bag all that was sweeped/policed and
dump it in the nearest empty container.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A719 HOSE OFF EXTERIOR PORCHES, WALKS AND STEPS The Contractor hoses off front and rear
porch areas and connecting steps to remove dirt, debris and leaves.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A720 CLEAN UNDERNEATH RAISED COMPUTER FLOORS The Contractor removes sufficient floor
tiles and vacuums all exposed wires and floor area. Tiles will be reset when work is complete.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A721 CLEAN PARK BENCHES The Contractor cleans park benches to remove dirt, leaves and
other matter so the benches look clean and not unsightly.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A722 UPHOLSTERED FURNITURE CLEANING The Contractor cleans upholstered furniture so they
are free of loose soil, debris, lint, dust, and other matter. All spots and stains will be
cleaned in the process.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A723 REMOVING SNOW AND ICE The Contractor removes snow and ice from those building walks
ad entrances so that these areas are clean and safe for pedestrian traffic, and maintains the
areas free of snow and ice until 1800. The Contractor does not deposit shoveled/blown snow and
ice on common sidewalks being cleared by other station activities under any circumstances.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A724 CLEANING OF VENTILATION DIFFUSERS, GRILLES, AND VENTS Provide cleaning of
ventilation diffusers, grilles and vents by wiping with clean, cloth towels and if necessary
the Contracctor shall incorporate the use of approved solvents and cleaners to obtain the
desired results. The cleaning process shall remove all exterior dirt, dust and other unwanted
materials. The finished surfaces shall not be damage or scratched as a result of the cleaning
process.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A725 WATER EXTRACTION The Contractor shall remove water from interior building surfaces
where flooding has occurred due to pipe leaks, roof leaks, toilet overflow, and other various
sources of water intrusion. The interior building surfaces include all floor finishes. Removal
of water shall be performed in the most expeditious manner, by manual or mechanical means. The
Contractor shall respond within four (4) hours of the order to proceed and work until the water
is removed. The Contractor shall provide drying fans in conjunction with water removal from all
carpeted surfaces and other surfaces as directed by the Contracting Officer.
The Contractor shall respond and be onsite ready to begin work within four hours after notice
to proceed. Work shall be completed within three calendar days.
A726 MOLD CLEANING Provide mold cleaning and removal (mold growth, mold stains, mold
odors) from wood and other cellulose-based building materials such as OSB board, drywall,
plaster, plywood, and ceiling tile as well as concrete and masonry surfaces such as bricks,

-- 43 of 66 --

blocks, and poured concrete walls and floors. Other surfaces may include pipe insulation and
heating, ventilation, air conditioning (HVAC) insulation and ductwork surfaces. The locations
include interior building surfaces such as offices, mechanical equipment rooms, crawl spaces,
above suspended ceiling surfaces. All cleaning methods and materials shall be in conformance
with existing enviromental regulations and procedures.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A727 PROVIDE AND OPERATE AIR SCRUBBERS FOR MOLD CLEANING OPERATIONS The Contractor shall
provide air scrubber equipment when requested. A typical air scrubber includes a blower
assembly complete with HEPA filter, activated carbon filters and may include a germicidal UV-C
light. Air scrubbers are approved for use in removal of asbestos, lead, chemical fumes and
biological contaminants. Each order shall require the operation of one air scrubber for a
period of twenty-four (24) continuous hours of use. the Contractor shall provide power cords
required to reach the nearest power outlet.
The Contracting Officer may request the relocation of the air scrubber equipment within the
same 24 hour period and at no additional cost to the Government. Relocation is defined as "an
adjacent or adjoining room on the same floor of the building."
The Contractor shall place the equipment within eight (8) hours after receipt of order.
A728 PRESSURE WASHING Provide pressure washing services for exterior building surfaces.
The equipment pressure requirements (PSI) shall be determined by the necessity of the surface
to be cleaned. Typically this item will be used, but not limited to, cleaning of concrete
sidewalks, walkways, steps, ship piers and building exterior finishes such as brick, vinyl,
wood, concrete, stucco, EIFS (Exterior Insulation Finishing System). This will also include the
cleaning of areas around trash dumpsters. When necessary, the contractor shall also be required
to use approved cleaning chemicals that can be dispensed along with the pressure washing
process. The Contractor will be permitted to use the most convenient fresh water source located
at the work site as directed by the KO. The Contractor shall be required to provide sufficient
non-metallic water hoses to reach the water source.
Work shall be completed within three calendar days after receipt of order.
A729 EMERGENCY CLEANING (Normal Working Hours) The Contractor shall provide emergency
cleaning services during normal working hours. Typical emergency cleaning services include
clean-up and removal of water from various surfaces due to plumbing or building leaks, removal
and clean up of broken ceiling tiles, broken glass, construction debris, dust, tracked in
mud/grease etc. The Contractor shall provide drying fans and other equipment as needed to
remove moisture from carpeting in a timely manner as to prevent mold growth and other damage
associated with moisture problems. Services may also include cleanup and removal of human
waste. This requirement will be noted on the order. The contractor shall perform the required
clean-up services at the same level as required for similar types of services set forth in
Spec. Item 3.1 of the Firm Fixed Price portion of the contract.
The Contractor shall respond within 1 hour after receipt of order and shall proceed until all
work is completed.
Services shall be ordered by the SF. Areas to be cleaned will be measured by the Government and
confirmed by the Contractor.
A730 EMERGENCY CLEANING (Other Than Normal Working Hours) The Contractor shall provide
emergency cleaning services during other than normal working hours. Typical emergency cleaning
services include clean-up and removal of water from various surfaces due to plumbing or
building leaks, removal and clean up of broken ceiling tiles, broken glass, construction
debris, dust, tracked in mud/grease etc. The Contractor shall provide drying fans and other
equipment as needed to remove the moisture from carpeting in a timely manner as to prevent mold
growth and other damage associated with moisture problems. Services may also include cleanup
and removal of human waste. This requirement will be noted on the order. The contractor shall

-- 44 of 66 --

perform the required clean-up services at the same level as required for similar types of
services set forth in Spec. Item 3.1 of the Firm Fixed Price portion of the contract.
The Contractor shall respond within 4 hours after receipt of order and shall proceed until all
work is completed.
Services shall be ordered by the SF. Areas to be cleaned will be measured by the Government and
confirmed by the Contractor.
A731 Disinfection of Frequently Touched Surfaces in Common Areas (Daily service for 30 day
period) The Contractor shall clean and disinfect fequently touched surfaces in common areas
to ensure surfaces are clean, sanitary, and free of potentially infectious materials. The
Contractor shall perform this task daily for a period of 30 days.
The Contractor shall clean and disinfect all frequently touched surfaces in common areas
(including lunch/break rooms), e.g., cabinets, chairs, copiers, countertops, doors, doorknobs,
handrails, elevator touch pads, ice machines, keyboards, light switches, microwave ovens,
monitors, phones, printers, refrigerators, shelving, shredders, tabletops, and vending
machines.
Common Areas include areas such as entryways, hallways, lobbies, lunch/break rooms, reception
areas, waiting rooms, conference rooms, elevators, and stairwells. >>
Surfaces shall be cleaned prior to disinfection, as instructed on the disinfectant
manufacturer s label. The Contractor shall ensure adequate contact time for effective
disinfection.
Cleaning agents used shall be EPA Approved for use against COVID-19. A list of EPA Approved
products is available at
https://www.epa.gov/pesticide-registration/list-n-disinfectants-use-against-sars-cov-2 or
https://www.americanchemistry.com/Novel-Coronavirus-Fighting-Products-List.pdf.
A732 Unit Priced Labor Work - MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide labor to perform all
Unit Priced Labor work subject to the Service Contract Act per the scope and delivery schedule
specified in the order.
A733 Unit Priced Labor Work - MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide labor to perform all
Unit Priced Labor work subject to the Collective Bargaining Agreement per the scope and
delivery schedule specified in the order.
A734 Material Costs- MUST BE NEGOTIATED BY KO. Provide all materials and equipment to
perform Unit Priced Labor work per the scope and delivery schedule specified in the order.
